        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





msm drm gpu driver ioctl handler msm_ioctl_gem_submit has a refcount leak bug. Affect several kernel versions, for chrome os kernels, it affects from v4.14 to v6.1. 



<span class="line"><!---->msm drm gpu driver ioctl handler msm_ioctl_gem_submit has a refcount leak bug. Affect several kernel versions, for chrome os kernels, it affects from v4.14 to v6.1. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In function msm_ioctl_gem_submit, it will call msm_submitqueue_get, msm_submitqueue_get will increase queue's refcount:



<span class="line"><!---->In function msm_ioctl_gem_submit, it will call msm_submitqueue_get, msm_submitqueue_get will increase queue's refcount:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





struct msm_gpu_submitqueue *msm_submitqueue_get(struct msm_file_private *ctx,



<span class="line"><!---->struct msm_gpu_submitqueue *msm_submitqueue_get(struct msm_file_private *ctx,<!----></span>



<br>





		u32 id)



<span class="line"><!---->		u32 id)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





	struct msm_gpu_submitqueue *entry;



<span class="line"><!---->	struct msm_gpu_submitqueue *entry;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	if (!ctx)



<span class="line"><!---->	if (!ctx)<!----></span>



<br>





		return NULL;



<span class="line"><!---->		return NULL;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	read_lock(&ctx->queuelock);



<span class="line"><!---->	read_lock(&amp;ctx-&gt;queuelock);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	list_for_each_entry(entry, &ctx->submitqueues, node) {



<span class="line"><!---->	list_for_each_entry(entry, &amp;ctx-&gt;submitqueues, node) {<!----></span>



<br>





		if (entry->id == id) {



<span class="line"><!---->		if (entry-&gt;id == id) {<!----></span>



<br>





			kref_get(&entry->ref);       <-------- increase refcount



<span class="line"><!---->			kref_get(&amp;entry-&gt;ref);       &lt;-------- increase refcount<!----></span>



<br>





			read_unlock(&ctx->queuelock);



<span class="line"><!---->			read_unlock(&amp;ctx-&gt;queuelock);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





			return entry;



<span class="line"><!---->			return entry;<!----></span>



<br>





		}



<span class="line"><!---->		}<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	read_unlock(&ctx->queuelock);



<span class="line"><!---->	read_unlock(&amp;ctx-&gt;queuelock);<!----></span>



<br>





	return NULL;



<span class="line"><!---->	return NULL;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





But in function msm_ioctl_gem_submit, error paths will not decrease the refcount, cause refcount leak. For example in function msm_ioctl_gem_submit:



<span class="line"><!---->But in function msm_ioctl_gem_submit, error paths will not decrease the refcount, cause refcount leak. For example in function msm_ioctl_gem_submit:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	queue = msm_submitqueue_get(ctx, args->queueid);



<span class="line"><!---->	queue = msm_submitqueue_get(ctx, args-&gt;queueid);<!----></span>



<br>





	if (!queue)



<span class="line"><!---->	if (!queue)<!----></span>



<br>





		return -ENOENT;



<span class="line"><!---->		return -ENOENT;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	ring = gpu->rb[queue->ring_nr];



<span class="line"><!---->	ring = gpu-&gt;rb[queue-&gt;ring_nr];<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	if (args->flags & MSM_SUBMIT_FENCE_FD_OUT) {



<span class="line"><!---->	if (args-&gt;flags &amp; MSM_SUBMIT_FENCE_FD_OUT) {<!----></span>



<br>





		out_fence_fd = get_unused_fd_flags(O_CLOEXEC);



<span class="line"><!---->		out_fence_fd = get_unused_fd_flags(O_CLOEXEC);<!----></span>



<br>





		if (out_fence_fd < 0) {



<span class="line"><!---->		if (out_fence_fd &lt; 0) {<!----></span>



<br>





			ret = out_fence_fd;



<span class="line"><!---->			ret = out_fence_fd;<!----></span>



<br>





			return ret;     <----------- return without dec refcount



<span class="line"><!---->			return ret;     &lt;----------- return without dec refcount<!----></span>



<br>





		}



<span class="line"><!---->		}<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	submit = submit_create(dev, gpu, queue, args->nr_bos, args->nr_cmds);



<span class="line"><!---->	submit = submit_create(dev, gpu, queue, args-&gt;nr_bos, args-&gt;nr_cmds);<!----></span>



<br>





	if (IS_ERR(submit))



<span class="line"><!---->	if (IS_ERR(submit))<!----></span>



<br>





		return PTR_ERR(submit);  <----------- return without dec refcount, If I input big args->nr_bos or nr_cmds will return ENOMEM error



<span class="line"><!---->		return PTR_ERR(submit);  &lt;----------- return without dec refcount, If I input big args-&gt;nr_bos or nr_cmds will return ENOMEM error<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





v5.15 code link:



<span class="line"><!---->v5.15 code link:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/chromiumos/codesearch/+/main:src/third_party/kernel/v5.15/drivers/gpu/drm/msm/msm_gem_submit.c;drc=b77c764b4371de0c34d23527ab507b195e90ce65;l=759



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/chromiumos/codesearch/+/main:src/third_party/kernel/v5.15/drivers/gpu/drm/msm/msm_gem_submit.c;drc=b77c764b4371de0c34d23527ab507b195e90ce65;l=759"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/chromiumos/codesearch/+/main:src/third_party/kernel/v5.15/drivers/gpu/drm/msm/msm_gem_submit.c;drc=b77c764b4371de0c34d23527ab507b195e90ce65;l=759<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Linux kernels, chrome os kernels, v4.14 to v6.1



<span class="line"><!---->Linux kernels, chrome os kernels, v4.14 to v6.1<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





I think this is an obvious problem from above code path, if you want a poc, just let me know.



<span class="line"><!---->I think this is an obvious problem from above code path, if you want a poc, just let me know.<!----></span>

Attachment is a PoC I run on my chromeos tablet which is Qualcomm 7C: 



<span class="line"><!---->Attachment is a PoC I run on my chromeos tablet which is Qualcomm 7C: <!----></span>



<br>





112.0.5616.62, wormdingler, strongbad



<span class="line"><!---->112.0.5616.62, wormdingler, strongbad<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The PoC will trigger msm_ioctl_gem_submit return error when submit_create kzalloc failed:



<span class="line"><!---->The PoC will trigger msm_ioctl_gem_submit return error when submit_create kzalloc failed:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	queue = msm_submitqueue_get(ctx, args->queueid);  <----------- kref_get



<span class="line"><!---->	queue = msm_submitqueue_get(ctx, args-&gt;queueid);  &lt;----------- kref_get<!----></span>



<br>





	if (!queue)



<span class="line"><!---->	if (!queue)<!----></span>



<br>





		return -ENOENT;



<span class="line"><!---->		return -ENOENT;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	ring = gpu->rb[queue->ring_nr];



<span class="line"><!---->	ring = gpu-&gt;rb[queue-&gt;ring_nr];<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	if (args->flags & MSM_SUBMIT_FENCE_FD_OUT) {



<span class="line"><!---->	if (args-&gt;flags &amp; MSM_SUBMIT_FENCE_FD_OUT) {<!----></span>



<br>





		out_fence_fd = get_unused_fd_flags(O_CLOEXEC);



<span class="line"><!---->		out_fence_fd = get_unused_fd_flags(O_CLOEXEC);<!----></span>



<br>





		if (out_fence_fd < 0) {



<span class="line"><!---->		if (out_fence_fd &lt; 0) {<!----></span>



<br>





			ret = out_fence_fd;



<span class="line"><!---->			ret = out_fence_fd;<!----></span>



<br>





			return ret;  



<span class="line"><!---->			return ret;  <!----></span>



<br>





		}



<span class="line"><!---->		}<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	submit = submit_create(dev, gpu, queue, args->nr_bos, args->nr_cmds);



<span class="line"><!---->	submit = submit_create(dev, gpu, queue, args-&gt;nr_bos, args-&gt;nr_cmds);<!----></span>



<br>





	if (IS_ERR(submit))



<span class="line"><!---->	if (IS_ERR(submit))<!----></span>



<br>





		return PTR_ERR(submit);  <----------- return without dec refcount, If I input big args->nr_bos or nr_cmds will return ENOMEM error



<span class="line"><!---->		return PTR_ERR(submit);  &lt;----------- return without dec refcount, If I input big args-&gt;nr_bos or nr_cmds will return ENOMEM error<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

FROMGIT: drm/msm: Fix submit error-path leaks



<span class="line"><!---->FROMGIT: drm/msm: Fix submit error-path leaks<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For errors after msm_submitqueue_get(), we need to drop the submitqueue



<span class="line"><!---->For errors after msm_submitqueue_get(), we need to drop the submitqueue<!----></span>



<br>





reference.  Additionally after get_unused_fd() we need to drop the fd.



<span class="line"><!---->reference.  Additionally after get_unused_fd() we need to drop the fd.<!----></span>



<br>





The ordering for dropping the queue lock and put_unused_fd() is not



<span class="line"><!---->The ordering for dropping the queue lock and put_unused_fd() is not<!----></span>



<br>





important, so just move this all into out_post_unlock.



<span class="line"><!---->important, so just move this all into out_post_unlock.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





v2: Only drop queue ref if submit doesn't take it



<span class="line"><!---->v2: Only drop queue ref if submit doesn't take it<!----></span>



<br>





v3: Fix unitialized submit ref in error path



<span class="line"><!---->v3: Fix unitialized submit ref in error path<!----></span>



<br>





v4: IS_ERR_OR_NULL()



<span class="line"><!---->v4: IS_ERR_OR_NULL()<!----></span>

How is this useful in an exploit? It looks like the ref count leak leaves the count larger rather than smaller so this might lead to a memory leak, but we don't treat availability issues as security bugs. Do we know if it is possible to get the refcount to over flow and allow for a use-after-free?



<span class="line"><!---->How is this useful in an exploit? It looks like the ref count leak leaves the count larger rather than smaller so this might lead to a memory leak, but we don't treat availability issues as security bugs. Do we know if it is possible to get the refcount to over flow and allow for a use-after-free?<!----></span>

Thank you for this report, lovepink. In VRP evaluation of this issue, it appears the refcount saturate would prevent an overflow and does not appear to be a security issue that would result in security consequences, therefore, this report is not eligible for a VRP reward. If you can provide a demonstration of this issue being exploited to result in user harm, please feel free to provide that and we would be happy to reassess for a potential VRP reward.



<span class="line"><!---->Thank you for this report, lovepink. In VRP evaluation of this issue, it appears the refcount saturate would prevent an overflow and does not appear to be a security issue that would result in security consequences, therefore, this report is not eligible for a VRP reward. If you can provide a demonstration of this issue being exploited to result in user harm, please feel free to provide that and we would be happy to reassess for a potential VRP reward.<!----></span>

          position: absolute;

          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
